Your good reviews are years old!
Now we know why.
Sunday 9/20/2015 10:30 am
CASH OR DEBIT CARD ONLY
Charging a "Merchant Fee" of $0.49 for using a debit card to pay without prior notice and attempts to hide the fact by not automatically giving a receipt and long delays in giving requested receipts.

Filthy, food covered floors and sticky crumb covered tables.

Demanding to know how many donuts I want to order no fewer than 9 times while we're discussing our order is rude. Telling your staff once "I'm not sure yet" should be plenty to send the message we weren't ready to order yet. Maybe I should have said you have nothing I actually want but I promised my toddler he could pick out a treat so I'm stuck buying atleast 1. Perhaps telling us about the donuts, like how you fill the jelly and custard donuts to order, or even what flavor jelly you offer, are we able to get any donut filled? Salesmenship goes along way to increasing order size.

My husband took our toddler to wash his hands while I looked over the case, menu boards, checked out the dirty tables and floor AND  back counter while a gal sprayed windex on the donut case. My family is very disappointed with the level of care given by Dr. Gil.

Our 15 year old dog needed a refill on a prescription flea medication. We made her an appointment, at which time Dr. John Gil informed us she needed a vaccine booster and prescribed her a blood pressure medication. Within 12 hours of her first medication dose and vaccine, our beloved family dog became very ill. She was unable to stand, panting excessively, and quite obviously unwell. We monitored her closely that night, and had to take her to an emergency veterinary hospital early the next morning. After almost two days in the hospital, we made the very difficult decision to put our dog to sleep.

Our family is devastated. Under the care of her prior vet, Dr. H at Alhambra Veterinary Hospital, all our family dogs have been healthy and happy. <response>None</response><Time>1525648617808<//Time>< text>
Ambiance :

Music was painfully loud and Im used to loud . They had a mariachi which I love but their speakers were blasting  to try to cover the music from their small bar in the next room. The bar was louder than any night club and it was just a very uncomfortable experience.  I walked out with a headache.

Food:

Mediocre .  They serves in big plates that are mainly 95% rice and beans.  The food is nothing  special and overpriced.  We had Shirmp al mojo de ajo and  it was undercooked and they used garlic seasoning instead of real garlic (8 small shrimps. I counted them). We ordered salad instead of rice and beans and don't have a single homemade dressing. The spicy  salsa was basically canned chipotle  chillies with some seasoning.  The bacon wrapped shrimp was okay... bacon was a little burned . The taquitos were okay and enchilada was just okay. Margaritas tasted like a lemonade kool-aid.

This place has so much potential the place it's really nice and  they have good menu but they lack  good chef and good management.<//text>

< Text>
The favorite item for me at this restaurant are the out of this world homemade flour tortillas.  Order some if you get the chance.   This place is large and well appointed.  The bar is separated from the dining area and features live music on some nights.  Since it was late when we arrived we shared some appetizers.
